The notice explains why we transferred your case. Please follow the instructions in the notice. If you do not receive your notice by January 15, 2023, please go to www.uscis.gov/e-request to request a copy of the notice. If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.

If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.
